Free Region, will leave the organization after a transition period in connection with the Company&#8217;s new regional structure and related senior management changes. Mr. Azinovic will continue to be employed by the Company until his separation on March 31, 2023. In connection with Mr. Azinovic&#8217;s departure, on February 27, 2023, the Company and Mr. Azinovic entered into a separation agreement and release (the &#8220;Separation Agreement&#8221;) with the following key terms, which are consistent with the applicable terms set forth in Mr. Azinovic&#8217;s employment agreement with Philip Morris International Management SA, effective August 1, 2012, and that certain Supplemental Letter to the Offer Letter with Drago Azinovic, dated December 4, 2008 (the &#8220;2008 Letter&#8221;), as previously disclosed by the Company:</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New employment, and he </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">will therefore receive a severance payment of CHF 2,401,909 (or $2,553,728</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New
